Smuggling Exploitation Plan

  • CL.TE: Backend may parse TE, proxy may use CL ‚Üí split request
  • TE.CL: Proxy parses TE, backend uses CL ‚Üí smuggled prefix
  • Double-CL: Ambiguity in length header can lead to desync
  • Malformed-TE: Unexpected Transfer-Encoding values may bypass filters
